function checkStalker(npc_community, gulag_type, npc_rank, se_obj)

    if gulag_type == "esc_freedom" then
    return npc_community == "freedom" or npc_community == "bandit" or npc_community == "stalker"
  end
    
  if gulag_type == "esc_tonnel" then
    return npc_community == "stalker" or npc_community == "bandit"
  end
  
  if gulag_type == "esc_smart" then
    return npc_community == "stalker"
  end
